    2332                 :         28 :             continue;
    2333                 :            : 
    2334                 :            :         // We should not consider coins which aren't at least in our mempool
    2335                 :            :         // It's possible for these to be conflicted via ancestors which we may never be able to detect
    2336 [ +  + ][ +  + ]:      93846 :         if (nDepth == 0 && !pcoin->InMempool())
    2337                 :        132 :             continue;
    2338                 :            : 
    2339                 :      93714 :         bool safeTx = pcoin->IsTrusted(locked_chain);
    2340                 :            : 
    2341                 :            :         // We should not consider coins from transactions that are replacing
    2342                 :            :         // other transactions.
    2343                 :            :         //
    2344                 :            :         // Example: There is a transaction A which is replaced by bumpfee
    2345                 :            :         // transaction B. In this case, we want to prevent creation of
    2346                 :            :         // a transaction B' which spends an output of B.
    2347                 :            :         //
    2348                 :            :         // Reason: If transaction A were initially confirmed, transactions B
    2349                 :            :         // and B' would no longer be valid, so the user would have to create
    2350                 :            :         // a new transaction C to replace B'. However, in the case of a
    2351                 :            :         // one-block reorg, transactions B' and C might BOTH be accepted,
    2352                 :            :         // when the user only wanted one of them. Specifically, there could
    2353                 :            :         // be a 1-block reorg away from the chain where transactions A and C

    2709                 :        653 : static uint32_t GetLocktimeForNewTransaction(interfaces::Chain& chain, interfaces::Chain::Lock& locked_chain)
    2710                 :            : {
    2711                 :        653 :     uint32_t const height = locked_chain.getHeight().get_value_or(-1);
    2712                 :            :     uint32_t locktime;
    2713                 :            :     // Discourage fee sniping.
    2714                 :            :     //
    2715                 :            :     // For a large miner the value of the transactions in the best block and
    2716                 :            :     // the mempool can exceed the cost of deliberately attempting to mine two
    2717                 :            :     // blocks to orphan the current best block. By setting nLockTime such that
    2718                 :            :     // only the next block can include the transaction, we discourage this
    2719                 :            :     // practice as the height restricted and limited blocksize gives miners
    2720                 :            :     // considering fee sniping fewer options for pulling off this attack.
    2721                 :            :     //
    2722                 :            :     // A simple way to think about this is from the wallet's point of view we
    2723                 :            :     // always want the blockchain to move forward. By setting nLockTime this
    2724                 :            :     // way we're basically making the statement that we only want this
    2725                 :            :     // transaction to appear in the next block; we don't want to potentially
    2726                 :            :     // encourage reorgs by allowing transactions to appear at lower heights
    2727                 :            :     // than the next block in forks of the best chain.
    2728                 :            :     //
    2729                 :            :     // Of course, the subsidy is high enough, and transaction volume low
    2730                 :            :     // enough, that fee sniping isn't a problem yet, but by implementing a fix
    2731                 :            :     // now we ensure code won't be written that makes assumptions about
    2732                 :            :     // nLockTime that preclude a fix later.
    2733         [ +  + ]:        653 :     if (IsCurrentForAntiFeeSniping(chain, locked_chain)) {
    2734                 :        652 :         locktime = height;
    2735                 :            : 
    2736                 :            :         // Secondly occasionally randomly pick a nLockTime even further back, so
    2737                 :            :         // that transactions that are delayed after signing for whatever reason,
    2738                 :            :         // e.g. high-latency mix networks and some CoinJoin implementations, have
    2739                 :            :         // better privacy.
    2740         [ +  + ]:        652 :         if (GetRandInt(10) == 0)
    2741                 :        130 :             locktime = std::max(0, (int)locktime - GetRandInt(100));
    2742                 :            :     } else {
    2743                 :            :         // If our chain is lagging behind, we can't discourage fee sniping nor help
    2744                 :            :         // the privacy of high-latency transactions. To avoid leaking a potentially
    2745                 :            :         // unique "nLockTime fingerprint", set nLockTime to a constant.
    2746                 :            :         locktime = 0;
    2747                 :            :     }
    2748         [ -  + ]:        653 :     assert(locktime <= height);
    2749         [ -  + ]:        653 :     assert(locktime < LOCKTIME_THRESHOLD);
    2750                 :        653 :     return locktime;
    2751                 :            : }

    3894                 :            :  *
    3895                 :            :  * Logic:
    3896                 :            :  * - If sending a transaction, assign its timestamp to the current time.
    3897                 :            :  * - If receiving a transaction outside a block, assign its timestamp to the
    3898                 :            :  *   current time.
